     name="het_CLEAN_TEXT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :local text $cleanInput;
         :if ([:len $text] = 0) do={
           :set cleanOutput "";
           :return;
         }
       
         :local repl do={
           :local src $1;
           :local findText $2;
           :local repText $3;
           :local pos [:find $src $findText];
           :while ($pos != nil) do={
             :set src ([:pick $src 0 $pos] . $repText . [:pick $src ($pos + [:len $findText]) [:len $src]]);
             :set pos [:find $src $findText];
           }
           :return $src;
         };
       
         :set text [$repl $text "%" "%25"];
         :set text [$repl $text " " "%20"];
         :set text [$repl $text "&" "%26"];
         :set text [$repl $text "?" "%3F"];
         :set text [$repl $text "=" "%3D"];
         :set text [$repl $text "+" "%2B"];
         :set text [$repl $text ";" "%3B"];
         :set text [$repl $text "|" "%7C"];
         :set text [$repl $text ":" "%3A"];
         :set text [$repl $text ">" "%3E"];
         :set text [$repl $text "<" "%3C"];
         :set text [$repl $text "#" "%23"];
       
         :set cleanOutput $text;

     name="het_PUSH_LOGS" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global logLimit;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastLogKey;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ids [/log find];
         :local total [:len $ids];
         :local idx 0;
         :local start 0;
         :local markerFound 0;
         :local afterMarker 0;
         :local newestKey "";
       
         :if ($total = 0) do={ :return; }
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] = 0) and ($total > $logLimit)) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
       
         :foreach id in=$ids do={
           :local logTime [/log get $id time];
           :local topics [/log get $id topics];
           :local msg [/log get $id message];
           :local key ($logTime . "|" . $topics . "|" . $msg);
           :local sev "INFO";
           :local safeLogTime "";
           :local safeTopics "";
           :local safeMsg "";
       
           :set newestKey $key;
           :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
           :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
           :set cleanInput $logTime;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $topics;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $msg;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
           :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
             :set newestKey $key;
             :continue;
           }
       
           :if ([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) do={
             :if ($key = $hetLastLogKey) do={
               :set markerFound 1;
               :set afterMarker 1;
             } else={
               :if ($afterMarker = 1) do={
                 :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
                 /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
               }
             }
           } else={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
           }
       
           :set idx ($idx + 1);
         }
       
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) and ($markerFound = 0)) do={
           :set idx 0;
           :set start 0;
           :if ($total > $logLimit) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
           :foreach id in=$ids do={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :local logTime [/log get $id time];
               :local topics [/log get $id topics];
               :local msg [/log get $id message];
               :local sev "INFO";
               :local safeLogTime "";
               :local safeTopics "";
               :local safeMsg "";
               :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
               :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
               :set cleanInput $logTime;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $topics;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $msg;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
               :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
                 :set idx ($idx + 1);
                 :continue;
               }
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
           }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $newestKey] > 0) do={ :set hetLastLogKey $newestKey; }

     name="het_AUDIT_CHANGES" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastScriptCount;
         :global hetLastSchedCount;
         :global hetLastRouteCount;
         :global hetLastFwCount;
         :global hetLastWanState;
         :global hetLastIdentity;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ident [/system identity get name];
         :local scriptCount [/system script print count-only];
         :local schedCount [/system scheduler print count-only];
         :local routeCount [/ip route print count-only];
         :local fwCount [/ip firewall filter print count-only];
         :local ifid [/interface find where name=$WANIF];
         :local wanState "unknown";
         :local badHetSched [/system scheduler print count-only where name~"het_" and disabled=yes];
       
         :if ([:len $ifid] > 0) do={
           :local wanDisabled [/interface get $ifid disabled];
           :local wanRunning [/interface get $ifid running];
           :if (($wanDisabled = false) and ($wanRunning = true)) do={ :set wanState "up"; } else={ :set wanState "down"; }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $hetLastIdentity] = 0) do={ :set hetLastIdentity $ident; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastScriptCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastSchedCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastRouteCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastFwCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastWanState] = 0) do={ :set hetLastWanState $wanState; }
       
         :if ($ident != $hetLastIdentity) do={
           :local details ("name " . $hetLastIdentity . " -> " . $ident);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=identity&action=changed");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastIdentity $ident;
         }
       
         :if ($scriptCount != $hetLastScriptCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastScriptCount . " -> " . $scriptCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=scripts&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount;
         }
       
         :if ($schedCount != $hetLastSchedCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastSchedCount . " -> " . $schedCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=schedulers&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount;
         }
       
         :if ($routeCount != $hetLastRouteCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastRouteCount . " -> " . $routeCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=network&item=routes&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount;
         }
       
         :if ($fwCount != $hetLastFwCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastFwCount . " -> " . $fwCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=security&item=firewall-filter&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount;
         }
       
         :if ($wanState != $hetLastWanState) do={
           :local details ($hetLastWanState . " -> " . $wanState);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=interface&item=" . $WANIF . "&action=state-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastWanState $wanState;
         }

       \t\t} on-error={

       \t\t}

       \t\t\t:set SENDOK 0;
       \t\t}

       \t\t\t\t/tool fetch url=$backupSendUrl check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       \t\t\t\t:set SENDOK 1;
       \t\t\t} on-error={
       \t\t\t\t:set SENDOK 0;
       \t\t\t}
       \t\t}
       \t}
       
       \t:if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_FAIL"; }

     name="het_PUSH_LIVE" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/07/2026 22:35:41 
     run-count=3 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local cpu [/system resource get cpu-load];
         :local memFree [/system resource get free-memory];
         :local memTot [/system resource get total-memory];
         :local mem 0;
         :local uptime [/system resource get uptime];
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local pubip "0.0.0.0";
         :local addrIds [/ip address find where interface=$WANIF and disabled=no];
       
         :if ($memTot > 0) do={ :set mem (100 - (($memFree * 100) / $memTot)); }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :if ([:len $addrIds] > 0) do={
           :local rawAddr "";
           :foreach addrId in=$addrIds do={
             :if ([:len $rawAddr] = 0) do={ :set rawAddr [/ip address get $addrId address]; }
           }
           :if ([:len $rawAddr] > 0) do={
             :local slashPos [:find $rawAddr "/"];
             :if ($slashPos != nil) do={ :set pubip [:pick $rawAddr 0 $slashPos]; } else={ :set pubip $rawAddr; }
           }
         }
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=live&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&status=ONLINE&message=router_live_ok");
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&cpu=" . $cpu . "&memory=" . $mem);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&uptime=" . $uptime);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&public_ip=" . $pubip);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&ipsec=" . $ipsec . "&isp=n/a");
         /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
       
         :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_PUSH_LIVE_FAIL"; }

     name="het_CLEAN_TEXT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :local text $cleanInput;
         :if ([:len $text] = 0) do={
           :set cleanOutput "";
           :return;
         }
       
         :local repl do={
           :local src $1;
           :local findText $2;
           :local repText $3;
           :local pos [:find $src $findText];
           :while ($pos != nil) do={
             :set src ([:pick $src 0 $pos] . $repText . [:pick $src ($pos + [:len $findText]) [:len $src]]);
             :set pos [:find $src $findText];
           }
           :return $src;
         };
       
         :set text [$repl $text "%" "%25"];
         :set text [$repl $text " " "%20"];
         :set text [$repl $text "&" "%26"];
         :set text [$repl $text "?" "%3F"];
         :set text [$repl $text "=" "%3D"];
         :set text [$repl $text "+" "%2B"];
         :set text [$repl $text ";" "%3B"];
         :set text [$repl $text "|" "%7C"];
         :set text [$repl $text ":" "%3A"];
         :set text [$repl $text ">" "%3E"];
         :set text [$repl $text "<" "%3C"];
         :set text [$repl $text "#" "%23"];
       
         :set cleanOutput $text;

     name="het_PUSH_LOGS" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global logLimit;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastLogKey;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ids [/log find];
         :local total [:len $ids];
         :local idx 0;
         :local start 0;
         :local markerFound 0;
         :local afterMarker 0;
         :local newestKey "";
       
         :if ($total = 0) do={ :return; }
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] = 0) and ($total > $logLimit)) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
       
         :foreach id in=$ids do={
           :local logTime [/log get $id time];
           :local topics [/log get $id topics];
           :local msg [/log get $id message];
           :local key ($logTime . "|" . $topics . "|" . $msg);
           :local sev "INFO";
           :local safeLogTime "";
           :local safeTopics "";
           :local safeMsg "";
       
           :set newestKey $key;
           :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
           :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
           :set cleanInput $logTime;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $topics;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $msg;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
           :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
             :set newestKey $key;
             :continue;
           }
       
           :if ([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) do={
             :if ($key = $hetLastLogKey) do={
               :set markerFound 1;
               :set afterMarker 1;
             } else={
               :if ($afterMarker = 1) do={
                 :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
                 /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
               }
             }
           } else={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
           }
       
           :set idx ($idx + 1);
         }
       
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) and ($markerFound = 0)) do={
           :set idx 0;
           :set start 0;
           :if ($total > $logLimit) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
           :foreach id in=$ids do={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :local logTime [/log get $id time];
               :local topics [/log get $id topics];
               :local msg [/log get $id message];
               :local sev "INFO";
               :local safeLogTime "";
               :local safeTopics "";
               :local safeMsg "";
               :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
               :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
               :set cleanInput $logTime;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $topics;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $msg;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
               :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
                 :set idx ($idx + 1);
                 :continue;
               }
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
           }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $newestKey] > 0) do={ :set hetLastLogKey $newestKey; }

     name="het_AUDIT_CHANGES" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastScriptCount;
         :global hetLastSchedCount;
         :global hetLastRouteCount;
         :global hetLastFwCount;
         :global hetLastWanState;
         :global hetLastIdentity;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ident [/system identity get name];
         :local scriptCount [/system script print count-only];
         :local schedCount [/system scheduler print count-only];
         :local routeCount [/ip route print count-only];
         :local fwCount [/ip firewall filter print count-only];
         :local ifid [/interface find where name=$WANIF];
         :local wanState "unknown";
         :local badHetSched [/system scheduler print count-only where name~"het_" and disabled=yes];
       
         :if ([:len $ifid] > 0) do={
           :local wanDisabled [/interface get $ifid disabled];
           :local wanRunning [/interface get $ifid running];
           :if (($wanDisabled = false) and ($wanRunning = true)) do={ :set wanState "up"; } else={ :set wanState "down"; }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $hetLastIdentity] = 0) do={ :set hetLastIdentity $ident; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastScriptCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastSchedCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastRouteCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastFwCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastWanState] = 0) do={ :set hetLastWanState $wanState; }
       
         :if ($ident != $hetLastIdentity) do={
           :local details ("name " . $hetLastIdentity . " -> " . $ident);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=identity&action=changed");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastIdentity $ident;
         }
       
         :if ($scriptCount != $hetLastScriptCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastScriptCount . " -> " . $scriptCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=scripts&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount;
         }
       
         :if ($schedCount != $hetLastSchedCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastSchedCount . " -> " . $schedCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=schedulers&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount;
         }
       
         :if ($routeCount != $hetLastRouteCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastRouteCount . " -> " . $routeCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=network&item=routes&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount;
         }
       
         :if ($fwCount != $hetLastFwCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastFwCount . " -> " . $fwCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=security&item=firewall-filter&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount;
         }
       
         :if ($wanState != $hetLastWanState) do={
           :local details ($hetLastWanState . " -> " . $wanState);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);

       \t} on-error={
       \t\t:set SENDOK 0;

       \t\t\t/tool fetch url=$sendUrl check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       \t\t\t:set SENDOK 1;
       \t\t} on-error={
       \t\t\t:set SENDOK 0;
       \t\t}
       \t}

       \t\t\t:set SENDOK 1;
       \t\t} on-error={
       \t\t\t:set SENDOK 0;
       \t\t}
       
       \t\t:if ($SENDOK != 1) do={
       \t\t\t:do {
       \t\t\t\t/tool fetch url=$backupSendUrl check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       \t\t\t\t:set SENDOK 1;
       \t\t\t} on-error={
       \t\t\t\t:set SENDOK 0;
       \t\t\t}
       \t\t}
       \t}
       
       \t:if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_FAIL"; }

     name="het_APPEND_IFACE_ENTRY" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test

         }

     name="het_PUSH_LIVE" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/07/2026 22:35:41 
     run-count=3 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local cpu [/system resource get cpu-load];
         :local memFree [/system resource get free-memory];
         :local memTot [/system resource get total-memory];
         :local mem 0;
         :local uptime [/system resource get uptime];
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local pubip "0.0.0.0";
         :local addrIds [/ip address find where interface=$WANIF and disabled=no];
       
         :if ($memTot > 0) do={ :set mem (100 - (($memFree * 100) / $memTot)); }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :if ([:len $addrIds] > 0) do={
           :local rawAddr "";
           :foreach addrId in=$addrIds do={
             :if ([:len $rawAddr] = 0) do={ :set rawAddr [/ip address get $addrId address]; }
           }
           :if ([:len $rawAddr] > 0) do={
             :local slashPos [:find $rawAddr "/"];
             :if ($slashPos != nil) do={ :set pubip [:pick $rawAddr 0 $slashPos]; } else={ :set pubip $rawAddr; }
           }
         }
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=live&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&status=ONLINE&message=router_live_ok");
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&cpu=" . $cpu . "&memory=" . $mem);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&uptime=" . $uptime);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&public_ip=" . $pubip);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&ipsec=" . $ipsec . "&isp=n/a");
         /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
       
         :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_PUSH_LIVE_FAIL"; }

     name="het_CLEAN_TEXT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :local text $cleanInput;
         :if ([:len $text] = 0) do={
           :set cleanOutput "";
           :return;
         }
       
         :local repl do={
           :local src $1;
           :local findText $2;
           :local repText $3;
           :local pos [:find $src $findText];
           :while ($pos != nil) do={
             :set src ([:pick $src 0 $pos] . $repText . [:pick $src ($pos + [:len $findText]) [:len $src]]);
             :set pos [:find $src $findText];
           }
           :return $src;
         };
       
         :set text [$repl $text "%" "%25"];
         :set text [$repl $text " " "%20"];
         :set text [$repl $text "&" "%26"];
         :set text [$repl $text "?" "%3F"];
         :set text [$repl $text "=" "%3D"];
         :set text [$repl $text "+" "%2B"];
         :set text [$repl $text ";" "%3B"];
         :set text [$repl $text "|" "%7C"];
         :set text [$repl $text ":" "%3A"];
         :set text [$repl $text ">" "%3E"];
         :set text [$repl $text "<" "%3C"];
         :set text [$repl $text "#" "%23"];
       
         :set cleanOutput $text;

     name="het_PUSH_LOGS" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global logLimit;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastLogKey;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ids [/log find];
         :local total [:len $ids];
         :local idx 0;
         :local start 0;
         :local markerFound 0;
         :local afterMarker 0;
         :local newestKey "";
       
         :if ($total = 0) do={ :return; }
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] = 0) and ($total > $logLimit)) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
       
         :foreach id in=$ids do={
           :local logTime [/log get $id time];
           :local topics [/log get $id topics];
           :local msg [/log get $id message];
           :local key ($logTime . "|" . $topics . "|" . $msg);
           :local sev "INFO";
           :local safeLogTime "";
           :local safeTopics "";
           :local safeMsg "";
       
           :set newestKey $key;
           :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
           :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
           :set cleanInput $logTime;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $topics;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $msg;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
           :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
             :set newestKey $key;
             :continue;
           }
       
           :if ([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) do={
             :if ($key = $hetLastLogKey) do={
               :set markerFound 1;
               :set afterMarker 1;
             } else={
               :if ($afterMarker = 1) do={
                 :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
                 /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
               }
             }
           } else={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
           }
       
           :set idx ($idx + 1);
         }
       
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) and ($markerFound = 0)) do={
           :set idx 0;
           :set start 0;
           :if ($total > $logLimit) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
           :foreach id in=$ids do={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :local logTime [/log get $id time];
               :local topics [/log get $id topics];
               :local msg [/log get $id message];
               :local sev "INFO";
               :local safeLogTime "";
               :local safeTopics "";
               :local safeMsg "";
               :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
               :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
               :set cleanInput $logTime;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $topics;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $msg;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
               :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
                 :set idx ($idx + 1);
                 :continue;
               }
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
           }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $newestKey] > 0) do={ :set hetLastLogKey $newestKey; }

     name="het_AUDIT_CHANGES" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastScriptCount;
         :global hetLastSchedCount;
         :global hetLastRouteCount;
         :global hetLastFwCount;
         :global hetLastWanState;
         :global hetLastIdentity;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ident [/system identity get name];
         :local scriptCount [/system script print count-only];
         :local schedCount [/system scheduler print count-only];
         :local routeCount [/ip route print count-only];
         :local fwCount [/ip firewall filter print count-only];
         :local ifid [/interface find where name=$WANIF];
         :local wanState "unknown";
         :local badHetSched [/system scheduler print count-only where name~"het_" and disabled=yes];
       
         :if ([:len $ifid] > 0) do={
           :local wanDisabled [/interface get $ifid disabled];
           :local wanRunning [/interface get $ifid running];
           :if (($wanDisabled = false) and ($wanRunning = true)) do={ :set wanState "up"; } else={ :set wanState "down"; }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $hetLastIdentity] = 0) do={ :set hetLastIdentity $ident; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastScriptCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastSchedCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastRouteCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastFwCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastWanState] = 0) do={ :set hetLastWanState $wanState; }
       
         :if ($ident != $hetLastIdentity) do={
           :local details ("name " . $hetLastIdentity . " -> " . $ident);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=identity&action=changed");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastIdentity $ident;
         }
       
         :if ($scriptCount != $hetLastScriptCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastScriptCount . " -> " . $scriptCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=scripts&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount;
         }
       
         :if ($schedCount != $hetLastSchedCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastSchedCount . " -> " . $schedCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=schedulers&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount;
         }
       
         :if ($routeCount != $hetLastRouteCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastRouteCount . " -> " . $routeCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=network&item=routes&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount;
         }
       
         :if ($fwCount != $hetLastFwCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastFwCount . " -> " . $fwCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=security&item=firewall-filter&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount;
         }
       
         :if ($wanState != $hetLastWanState) do={
           :local details ($hetLastWanState . " -> " . $wanState);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=interface&item=" . $WANIF . "&action=state-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastWanState $wanState;
         }
       
         :if ($badHetSched > 0) do={
           :set cleanInput "one or more het schedulers disabled";
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=monitoring&item=het_scheduler&action=disabled");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
         }

Flags: I - invalid 
     name="het_PUSH_LOGS" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global logLimit;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastLogKey;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ids [/log find];
         :local total [:len $ids];
         :local idx 0;
         :local start 0;
         :local markerFound 0;
         :local afterMarker 0;
         :local newestKey "";
       
         :if ($total = 0) do={ :return; }
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] = 0) and ($total > $logLimit)) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
       
         :foreach id in=$ids do={
           :local logTime [/log get $id time];
           :local topics [/log get $id topics];
           :local msg [/log get $id message];
           :local key ($logTime . "|" . $topics . "|" . $msg);
           :local sev "INFO";
           :local safeLogTime "";
           :local safeTopics "";
           :local safeMsg "";
       
           :set newestKey $key;
           :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
           :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
           :set cleanInput $logTime;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $topics;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
           :set cleanInput $msg;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
           :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
             :set newestKey $key;
             :continue;
           }
       
           :if ([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) do={
             :if ($key = $hetLastLogKey) do={
               :set markerFound 1;
               :set afterMarker 1;
             } else={
               :if ($afterMarker = 1) do={
                 :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
                 :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
                 /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
               }
             }
           } else={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
           }
       
           :set idx ($idx + 1);
         }
       
         :if (([:len $hetLastLogKey] > 0) and ($markerFound = 0)) do={
           :set idx 0;
           :set start 0;
           :if ($total > $logLimit) do={ :set start ($total - $logLimit); }
           :foreach id in=$ids do={
             :if ($idx >= $start) do={
               :local logTime [/log get $id time];
               :local topics [/log get $id topics];
               :local msg [/log get $id message];
               :local sev "INFO";
               :local safeLogTime "";
               :local safeTopics "";
               :local safeMsg "";
               :if (([:find $topics "critical"] != nil) or ([:find $topics "error"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "CRITICAL"; }
               :if (($sev = "INFO") and ([:find $topics "warning"] != nil)) do={ :set sev "HIGH"; }
               :set cleanInput $logTime;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeLogTime $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $topics;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeTopics $cleanOutput;
               :set cleanInput $msg;
               /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
               :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
               :if ([:find $msg "het_"] != nil) do={
                 :set idx ($idx + 1);
                 :continue;
               }
               :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=routerlog&site=" . $SITE);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&log_time=" . $safeLogTime);
               :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&topics=" . $safeTopics . "&severity=" . $sev . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
               /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
             }
             :set idx ($idx + 1);
           }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $newestKey] > 0) do={ :set hetLastLogKey $newestKey; }

     name="het_AUDIT_CHANGES" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetLastScriptCount;
         :global hetLastSchedCount;
         :global hetLastRouteCount;
         :global hetLastFwCount;
         :global hetLastWanState;
         :global hetLastIdentity;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local ident [/system identity get name];
         :local scriptCount [/system script print count-only];
         :local schedCount [/system scheduler print count-only];
         :local routeCount [/ip route print count-only];
         :local fwCount [/ip firewall filter print count-only];
         :local ifid [/interface find where name=$WANIF];
         :local wanState "unknown";
         :local badHetSched [/system scheduler print count-only where name~"het_" and disabled=yes];
       
         :if ([:len $ifid] > 0) do={
           :local wanDisabled [/interface get $ifid disabled];
           :local wanRunning [/interface get $ifid running];
           :if (($wanDisabled = false) and ($wanRunning = true)) do={ :set wanState "up"; } else={ :set wanState "down"; }
         }
       
         :if ([:len $hetLastIdentity] = 0) do={ :set hetLastIdentity $ident; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastScriptCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastSchedCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastRouteCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastFwCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastWanState] = 0) do={ :set hetLastWanState $wanState; }
       
         :if ($ident != $hetLastIdentity) do={
           :local details ("name " . $hetLastIdentity . " -> " . $ident);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=identity&action=changed");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastIdentity $ident;
         }
       
         :if ($scriptCount != $hetLastScriptCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastScriptCount . " -> " . $scriptCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=scripts&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount;
         }
       
         :if ($schedCount != $hetLastSchedCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastSchedCount . " -> " . $schedCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=schedulers&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount;
         }
       
         :if ($routeCount != $hetLastRouteCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastRouteCount . " -> " . $routeCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=network&item=routes&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount;
         }
       
         :if ($fwCount != $hetLastFwCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastFwCount . " -> " . $fwCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=security&item=firewall-filter&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount;
         }
       
         :if ($wanState != $hetLastWanState) do={
           :local details ($hetLastWanState . " -> " . $wanState);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=interface&item=" . $WANIF . "&action=state-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastWanState $wanState;
         }
       
         :if ($badHetSched > 0) do={
           :set cleanInput "one or more het schedulers disabled";
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=monitoring&item=het_scheduler&action=disabled");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
         }

         :global SITE;

         :global WANIF;

         :global hetLastSchedCount;

         :local schedCount [/system scheduler print count-only];
         :local routeCount [/ip route print count-only];
         :local fwCount [/ip firewall filter print count-only];

         :if ([:len $hetLastSchedCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastRouteCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastFwCount] = 0) do={ :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount; }
         :if ([:len $hetLastWanState] = 0) do={ :set hetLastWanState $wanState; }

           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=identity&action=changed");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastIdentity $ident;
         }
       
         :if ($scriptCount != $hetLastScriptCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastScriptCount . " -> " . $scriptCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=scripts&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastScriptCount $scriptCount;
         }
       
         :if ($schedCount != $hetLastSchedCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastSchedCount . " -> " . $schedCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=schedulers&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastSchedCount $schedCount;
         }
       
         :if ($routeCount != $hetLastRouteCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastRouteCount . " -> " . $routeCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=network&item=routes&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastRouteCount $routeCount;
         }
       
         :if ($fwCount != $hetLastFwCount) do={
           :local details ($hetLastFwCount . " -> " . $fwCount);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=security&item=firewall-filter&action=count-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastFwCount $fwCount;
         }
       
         :if ($wanState != $hetLastWanState) do={
           :local details ($hetLastWanState . " -> " . $wanState);
           :set cleanInput $details;
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=interface&item=" . $WANIF . "&action=state-change");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetLastWanState $wanState;
         }
       
         :if ($badHetSched > 0) do={
           :set cleanInput "one or more het schedulers disabled";
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=monitoring&item=het_scheduler&action=disabled");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
         }

     name="het_BOOT_EVENT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no run-count=0 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global hetBootSent;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
         :if ($hetBootSent != 1) do={
           :set cleanInput "router reboot or reinstall detected";
           /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
           :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=change&site=" . $SITE);
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&category=system&item=boot&action=startup");
           :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&details=" . $cleanOutput);
           /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
           :set hetBootSent 1;
         }

     name="het_HTTP_SEND" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:07:17 
     run-count=2 source=
       
       :global APIURL;
       :global BACKUPURL;
       :global SENDDATA;
       :global SENDOK;
       
       :if ([:len $APIURL] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
       :set SENDOK 0;
       :if ([:len $SENDDATA] = 0) do={
       :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_DATA_EMPTY";
       :return;
       }
       
       :do {
       /tool fetch url=$APIURL http-method=post http-data=$SENDDATA http-header-field="Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded" check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       :set SENDOK 1;
       } on-error={
       :set SENDOK 0;
       }
       
       :if (($SENDOK != 1) and ([:len $BACKUPURL] > 0)) do={
       :do {
       /tool fetch url=$BACKUPURL http-method=post http-data=$SENDDATA http-header-field="Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded" check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       :set SENDOK 1;
       } on-error={
       :set SENDOK 0;
       }
       }
       
       :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_FAIL"; }

     name="het_CLEAN_TEXT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:50:27 
     run-count=15 source=
       
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :local text $cleanInput;
         :if ([:len $text] = 0) do={
           :set cleanOutput "";
           :return;
         }
       
         :local repl do={
           :local src $1;
           :local findText $2;
           :local repText $3;
           :local pos [:find $src $findText];
           :while ($pos != nil) do={
             :set src ([:pick $src 0 $pos] . $repText . [:pick $src ($pos + [:len $findText]) [:len $src]]);
             :set pos [:find $src $findText];
           }
           :return $src;
         };
       
         :set text [$repl $text "%" "%25"];
         :set text [$repl $text " " "%20"];
         :set text [$repl $text "&" "%26"];
         :set text [$repl $text "" "%3F"];
         :set text [$repl $text "=" "%3D"];
         :set text [$repl $text "+" "%2B"];
         :set text [$repl $text ";" "%3B"];
         :set text [$repl $text "|" "%7C"];
         :set text [$repl $text ":" "%3A"];
         :set text [$repl $text ">" "%3E"];
         :set text [$repl $text "<" "%3C"];
         :set text [$repl $text "#" "%23"];
       
         :set cleanOutput $text;

     name="het_PUSH_LIVE" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:50:26 
     run-count=8 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local cpu [/system resource get cpu-load];
         :local memFree [/system resource get free-memory];
         :local memTot [/system resource get total-memory];
         :local mem 0;
         :local uptime [/system resource get uptime];
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local pubip "0.0.0.0";
         :local addrIds [/ip address find where interface=$WANIF and disabled=no];
         :local safeUptime "";
         :local safePubip "";
       
         :if ($memTot > 0) do={ :set mem (100 - (($memFree * 100) / $memTot)); }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :if ([:len $addrIds] > 0) do={
           :local rawAddr "";
           :foreach addrId in=$addrIds do={
             :if ([:len $rawAddr] = 0) do={ :set rawAddr [/ip address get $addrId address]; }
           }
           :if ([:len $rawAddr] > 0) do={
             :local slashPos [:find $rawAddr "/"];
             :if ($slashPos != nil) do={ :set pubip [:pick $rawAddr 0 $slashPos]; } else={ :set pubip $rawAddr; }
           }
         }
       
         :set cleanInput $uptime;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeUptime $cleanOutput;
         :set cleanInput $pubip;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safePubip $cleanOutput;
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=live&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&status=ONLINE&message=router_live_ok");
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&cpu=" . $cpu . "&memory=" . $mem);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&uptime=" . $safeUptime);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&public_ip=" . $safePubip);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&ipsec=" . $ipsec . "&isp=n/a");
         /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
       
         :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_PUSH_LIVE_FAIL"; }

     name="het_VPN_CHECK" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:45:30 
     run-count=5 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global VPNHOST;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local pingOk [/ping $VPNHOST count=2 interval=300ms];
         :local status "DOWN";
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local safeHost "";
         :local safeMsg "";
       
         :if ($pingOk > 0) do={ :set status "UP"; }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :set cleanInput $VPNHOST;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeHost $cleanOutput;
         :set cleanInput ("ipsec=" . $ipsec);
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=vpn&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&host=" . $safeHost);

     name="het_CONFIG" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:49:44 
     run-count=4 source=
       
       :global APIURL "https://mikrotik-monitor-proxy.hetgraphic17.workers.dev";
       :global BACKUPURL "";
       :global TOKEN "MONITOR_TOKEN_2026";
       :global SITE "KANO";
       :global ROUTER "AMBARIYYA_GLOBAL";
       :global WANIF "ether1";
       :global VPNHOST "vpn.hetdubai.com";
       :global SENDDATA "";
       :global SENDOK 0;
       :log info "het_CONFIG_LOADED";

     name="het_HTTP_SEND" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:07:17 
     run-count=2 source=
       
       :global APIURL;
       :global BACKUPURL;
       :global SENDDATA;
       :global SENDOK;
       
       :if ([:len $APIURL] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
       :set SENDOK 0;
       :if ([:len $SENDDATA] = 0) do={
       :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_DATA_EMPTY";
       :return;
       }
       
       :do {
       /tool fetch url=$APIURL http-method=post http-data=$SENDDATA http-header-field="Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded" check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       :set SENDOK 1;
       } on-error={
       :set SENDOK 0;
       }
       
       :if (($SENDOK != 1) and ([:len $BACKUPURL] > 0)) do={
       :do {
       /tool fetch url=$BACKUPURL http-method=post http-data=$SENDDATA http-header-field="Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded" check-certificate=no duration=10s output=none;
       :set SENDOK 1;
       } on-error={
       :set SENDOK 0;
       }
       }
       
       :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_HTTP_SEND_FAIL"; }

     name="het_CLEAN_TEXT" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:50:27 
     run-count=15 source=
       
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :local text $cleanInput;
         :if ([:len $text] = 0) do={
           :set cleanOutput "";
           :return;
         }
       
         :local repl do={
           :local src $1;
           :local findText $2;
           :local repText $3;
           :local pos [:find $src $findText];
           :while ($pos != nil) do={
             :set src ([:pick $src 0 $pos] . $repText . [:pick $src ($pos + [:len $findText]) [:len $src]]);
             :set pos [:find $src $findText];
           }
           :return $src;
         };
       
         :set text [$repl $text "%" "%25"];
         :set text [$repl $text " " "%20"];
         :set text [$repl $text "&" "%26"];
         :set text [$repl $text "" "%3F"];
         :set text [$repl $text "=" "%3D"];
         :set text [$repl $text "+" "%2B"];
         :set text [$repl $text ";" "%3B"];
         :set text [$repl $text "|" "%7C"];
         :set text [$repl $text ":" "%3A"];
         :set text [$repl $text ">" "%3E"];
         :set text [$repl $text "<" "%3C"];
         :set text [$repl $text "#" "%23"];
       
         :set cleanOutput $text;

     name="het_PUSH_LIVE" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:50:26 
     run-count=8 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global WANIF;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local cpu [/system resource get cpu-load];
         :local memFree [/system resource get free-memory];
         :local memTot [/system resource get total-memory];
         :local mem 0;
         :local uptime [/system resource get uptime];
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local pubip "0.0.0.0";
         :local addrIds [/ip address find where interface=$WANIF and disabled=no];
         :local safeUptime "";
         :local safePubip "";
       
         :if ($memTot > 0) do={ :set mem (100 - (($memFree * 100) / $memTot)); }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :if ([:len $addrIds] > 0) do={
           :local rawAddr "";
           :foreach addrId in=$addrIds do={
             :if ([:len $rawAddr] = 0) do={ :set rawAddr [/ip address get $addrId address]; }
           }
           :if ([:len $rawAddr] > 0) do={
             :local slashPos [:find $rawAddr "/"];
             :if ($slashPos != nil) do={ :set pubip [:pick $rawAddr 0 $slashPos]; } else={ :set pubip $rawAddr; }
           }
         }
       
         :set cleanInput $uptime;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeUptime $cleanOutput;
         :set cleanInput $pubip;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safePubip $cleanOutput;
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=live&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&status=ONLINE&message=router_live_ok");
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&cpu=" . $cpu . "&memory=" . $mem);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&uptime=" . $safeUptime);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&public_ip=" . $safePubip);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&ipsec=" . $ipsec . "&isp=n/a");
         /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
       
         :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_PUSH_LIVE_FAIL"; }

     name="het_VPN_CHECK" owner="asif" policy=read,write,policy,test 
     dont-require-permissions=no last-started=mar/08/2026 00:45:30 
     run-count=5 source=
       
         :global TOKEN;
         :global SITE;
         :global ROUTER;
         :global VPNHOST;
         :global SENDDATA;
         :global SENDOK;
         :global cleanInput;
         :global cleanOutput;
       
         :if ([:len $TOKEN] = 0) do={ /system script run het_CONFIG; }
       
         :local pingOk [/ping $VPNHOST count=2 interval=300ms];
         :local status "DOWN";
         :local peers 0;
         :local ipsec "DOWN";
         :local safeHost "";
         :local safeMsg "";
       
         :if ($pingOk > 0) do={ :set status "UP"; }
         :do { :set peers [/ip ipsec active-peers print count-only]; } on-error={ :set peers 0; };
         :if ($peers > 0) do={ :set ipsec "UP"; }
       
         :set cleanInput $VPNHOST;
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeHost $cleanOutput;
         :set cleanInput ("ipsec=" . $ipsec);
         /system script run het_CLEAN_TEXT;
         :set safeMsg $cleanOutput;
       
         :set SENDDATA ("token=" . $TOKEN . "&type=vpn&site=" . $SITE);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&router=" . $ROUTER . "&host=" . $safeHost);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&status=" . $status . "&ping=" . $pingOk);
         :set SENDDATA ($SENDDATA . "&message=" . $safeMsg);
         /system script run het_HTTP_SEND;
       
         :if ($SENDOK != 1) do={ :log error "het_VPN_CHECK_FAIL"; }
